cspks_req_wrapper :: DECLARE 
   l_source           cotms_source.source_code%TYPE := Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_source; 
   l_function_id      smtbs_menu.function_id%TYPE :=Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_function_id;
   l_source_operation VARCHAR2(100) := Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_source_operation; 
   l_action_code      VARCHAR2(50) := Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_action_code;  
   l_Exchange_Pattern VARCHAR2(4) := Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_Exchange_Pattern;  
   l_multi_trip_id    VARCHAR2(100) := Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_multi_trip_id; 
   l_Request_No       NUMBER := Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_Request_No; 
   l_addl_info        Cspks_Req_Global.ty_addl_info := Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_addl_info;
   l_status           VARCHAR2(50) := Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_status;
   l_err_code         VARCHAR2(32767) := Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_err_code; 
   l_err_params       VARCHAR2(32767) := Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_err_params;  
BEGIN
IF NOT Clpks_Cldacaut_Main.Fn_Process_Request(l_source,
l_source_operation,
l_function_id,
l_action_code,
l_Exchange_Pattern,
l_multi_trip_id,
l_Request_No,
l_addl_info,
l_status,
l_err_code,
l_err_params) THEN
Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_return := FALSE;
debug.pr_debug('ST','Failed in Clpks_Cldacaut_Main.Fn_Process_Request');
END IF;
   Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_source           := l_source; 
   Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_function_id      := l_function_id;
   Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_source_operation := l_source_operation; 
   Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_action_code      := l_action_code;  
   Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_Exchange_Pattern := l_Exchange_Pattern;  
   Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_multi_trip_id    := l_multi_trip_id; 
   Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_Request_No       := l_Request_No; 
   Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_addl_info        := l_addl_info;
   Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_status           := l_status;
   Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_err_code         := l_err_code; 
   Cspks_Req_Wrapper.g_err_params       := l_err_params;   
END;
